#		example_effect = yes
#	}

effect_play_as_ruler_set_target_on_them = {
	random_owned_leader = {
		limit = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
		}
		save_event_target_as = ruler
	}
}

effect_play_as_ruler_hobby_event_ended = {
	random_owned_leader = {
		limit = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
		}
		save_event_target_as = ruler
	}
	event_target:ruler = {
		set_timed_leader_flag = { flag = play_as_ruler_hobby_event_cooldown days = 720 }
	}
}

effect_play_as_ruler_gain_exp = {
	random_owned_leader = {
		limit = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
		}
		save_event_target_as = ruler
	}
	event_target:ruler = {
#		change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_exp value = 1 }
	}
}

effect_play_as_ruler_gain_ruled_time = {
	random_owned_leader = {
		limit = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
		}
		save_event_target_as = ruler
	}
	event_target:ruler = {
		change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_ruled_time value = 1 }
	}
}

effect_play_as_ruler_gain_campaign_exp = {
	random_owned_leader = {
		limit = {
			leader_class = ruler
			has_leader_flag = play_as_ruler_ruler_itself
		}
		save_event_target_as = ruler
	}
	change_variable = { which = play_as_ruler_campaign_exp value = 1 }
}

                which = rls_ruler_affair_level

        }
    }

                value < 0
            }
        }
        set_variable = {
            which = rls_ruler_idea_level
            value = 0
        }
    }
    clear_variable = rls_ruler_base_level_num

effect_play_as_ruler_set_category_num_cap = {
    leader = {
        set_variable = { #How many that can foci at a time, base is 3
            which = rls_ruler_category_num_cap
            value = 3
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    which = rls_ruler_affair_level
                    value >= 50
                }
            }
            change_variable = {
                which = rls_ruler_category_num_cap
                value = 1
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    which = rls_ruler_affair_level
                    value >= 70
                }
            }
            change_variable = {
                which = rls_ruler_category_num_cap
                value = 1
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    which = rls_ruler_affair_level
                    value >= 90
                }
            }
            change_variable = {
                which = rls_ruler_category_num_cap
                value = 1
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                check_variable = {
                    which = rls_ruler_affair_level
                    value >= 100
                }
            }
            change_variable = {
                which = rls_ruler_category_num_cap
                value = 1
            }
        }
    }
}

effect_play_as_ruler_non_ruler_level_their_foci = {
    switch = {
        trigger = has_ruler_trait
        trait_ruler_hobby_election_agrarian = {
            random_list = {
                1 = {
                    modifier = {
                        factor = 0
                        has_leader_flag = rls_agrarian_1_4_selected
                    }
                    
                    
                    
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            has_leader_flag = rls_agrarian_1_3_selected
                            NOT = {
                                has_leader_flag = rls_agrarian_1_4_selected
                            }
                        }
                        set_leader_flag = rls_agrarian_1_4_selected
                        
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            has_leader_flag = rls_agrarian_1_2_selected
                            NOT = {
                                has_leader_flag = rls_agrarian_1_3_selected
                            }
                        }

                            }
                        }
                        set_leader_flag = rls_agrarian_1_2_selected
                        
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            NOT = {
                                has_leader_flag = rls_agrarian_1_1_selected
                            }
                        }
                        set_leader_flag = rls_agrarian_1_1_selected
